TEST 03: 1993 Q2 establishment threshold chain
====================================================================================================
Category: numeric_threshold_chain
Expected note: Higher establishment thresholds should be contained in lower establishment thresholds. >=50 may be empty.

success: True | proof_type: live_database_except_pairwise | checked_on_current_database: True
limitations: Live-database check only. Not-contained and incomparable results are backed by counterexample rows. Contained/equivalent results are only verified on the current database, not as full symbolic proofs.

INPUT QUERIES
  Q1: Which areas had at least 20 agriculture, forestry, fishing, and hunting establishments in the second quarter of 1993?
  Q2: Which areas had at least 10 agriculture, forestry, fishing, and hunting establishments in the second quarter of 1993?

  Q4: Which areas had at least 50 agriculture, forestry, fishing, and hunting establishments in the second quarter of 1993?

GENERATED SQL / QUERY RESULTS
Q1. Which areas had at least 20 agriculture, forestry, fishing, and hunting establishments in the second quarter of 1993?
   success: True | safe: True | rows: 0 | empty: True
   columns: ['geoid', 'total_estabs']
   sql: SELECT "t_1993_q2"."geoid", SUM("t_1993_q2"."qtrly_estabs_11_agriculture_forestry_fishing_and_hunting") AS "total_estabs" FROM "t_1993_q2" GROUP BY "t_1993_q2"."geoid" HAVING "total_estabs" >= ?
Q2. Which areas had at least 10 agriculture, forestry, fishing, and hunting establishments in the second quarter of 1993?

   sql: WITH yearly_avg AS (   SELECT AVG(qtrly_estabs_11_agriculture_forestry_fishing_and_hunting) AS avg_val   FROM t_1990_q1   UNION ALL   SELECT AVG(qtrly_estabs_11_agriculture_forestry_fishing_and_hunting)   FROM t_1990_q2   UNION ALL   SELECT AVG(qtrly_estabs_11_agriculture_forestry_fishing_and_hunting)   FROM t_1990_q3   UNION ALL   SELECT AVG(qtrly_estabs_11_agriculture_forestry_fishing_and_hunting)   FROM t_1990_q4 ), combined AS (   SELECT geoid, qtrly_estabs_11_agriculture_forestry_fishing_and_hunting AS val FROM t_1990_q1   UNION ALL   SELECT geoid, qtrly_estabs_11_agriculture_forestry_fishing_and_hunting FROM t_1990_q2   UNION ALL   SELECT geoid, qtrly_estabs_11_agriculture_forestry_fishing_and_hunting FROM t_1990_q3   UNION ALL   SELECT geoid, qtrly_estabs_11_agriculture_forestry_fishing_and_hunting FROM t_1990_q4 ), geoid_quarters AS (   SELECT c.geoid, c.val, y.avg_val   FROM combined c   CROSS JOIN (SELECT AVG(val) AS avg_val FROM combined) y ), below_avg_geoids AS (   SELECT geoid   FROM geoid_quarters   WHERE val < avg_val   GROUP BY geoid   HAVING COUNT(*) = 4 ) SELECT DISTINCT t1.geoid FROM t_1990_q1 t1 JOIN t_1990_q2 t2 ON t1.geoid = t2.geoid JOIN t_1990_q3 t3 ON t1.geoid = t3.geoid JOIN t_1990_q4 t4 ON t1.geoid = t4.geoid WHERE t1.geoid IN (SELECT geoid FROM below_avg_geoids)
